 New Zealand captain Amy Sutthervat scored two consecutive half-centuries against India and has now reached the fourth position
 aswin ne bayaan kiya dard- chotil hone se breadman-sachin bhi nahin batch paenujiland kii purv captain suji bets ko bhi ek sthaan kaa phayda hua he
 Bates, who hit a half-century at Hamilton, now ranks sixth
 gendbaaji ranking main bhartiya gendbaaj dipti sharma, punam yadav or ekta bisht ke liye acchhee khabar he
 Deepti and Poonam have gone up five places each to reach 8th and 9th positions respectively
 punam ne newjiland ke khilaaf siries main chah wicket apane naam kiye the, jabaki dipti ne chaar wicket apane naam kiye the
 Ekta Bisht, who took five wickets in the series, has moved up nine places and is now ranked 13th
 duusare vanade main 23 ran dekar teen wicket lene vaali anbhavi tej gendbaaj bowlar jhulan goswami ko bhi ek sthaan kaa phayda hua he or ab vah chauthe paaydaan par hai
 Jhulan tops the Indian bowlers in the women's rankings, having managed to make it to the top-5
 gendbaaji main jhulan se upar jo teen khilaadi hai unamem pakistan kii sanaa mir, australia kii megan scat or dakshin africa marijen cap kaa naam he
 Negotiations on one side, firing on the other
 ye sachai keval bharat-pakistan kii hi nahin he
 There are many countries in the world which came into existence after partition
 lekin lagbhag ek hi phija main saans lene vaale, kabhi ek hi raashtragan gane vaale, ek hi jhande ko salaami dene vaale, dharti par lakeer khinchate hi ekaek dushman ban gaye
 One look at those countries whose fate is similar to india-pakistan relationship
 1
 With the surrender of Japan after the Second World War, Korea became independent of Japanese rule
 tab sanyukt raashtra ne prashasan ke liye ek trustiship yojana banaai jiske tahat korian peninsula ko 38wein samanaantar par do hisson main baant diya gaya
 The administration of North Korea was entrusted with the administration of the Soviet Union and South Korea to the USA
 june 1950 main soviet sangh kii shah par korian yuddh hua jo sangharsh viraam samjhaute par khatm hua
 Since then, as soon as efforts for reconciliation between the two countries intensify, guns are also fired on the border
 2
 russia-ukraine Prior to the Ukraine revolution of 21 February 2014, Russia and Ukraine had a better relationship during the reign of President Viktor Yanukovych
 cremia par adhikaar ko lekar donon deshon ke bich tanaav paidaa hua
 In March 2014, Russia captured Crimea on the pretext of a disputed referendum
 ye donon soviet sangh kaa hissaa the
 Now the relationship between them has become so bad that
 ukraine ne roosi sarhad par 'project wal' ke tahat lambii diwaar banani shuru kar di he
 3
 israel-philstinmai 1948 main philstin main based yahudiyon ne swatantraaa kaa elaan karte hue israel naam ke desh kaa elaan kar diya
 The very next day, Arab countries - Egypt, Jordan, Syria, Lebanon and Iraq - attacked Israel together
 ise 1948 kaa yuddh kaa naam diya gaya or yahi searab-israel yuki shuruyaat hui
 4
 eritrea or ithiopiahalanki eritrea or ithiopia vibhaajan ke baad astitv main nahin aae
 But to be separated from Ethiopia had to resort to referendum
 darasal, duusare vishwa yuddh se pehle purvottar africa desh eritrea par italy or phir britain kaa shashan tha
 In 1952, the United Nations made Ethiopia a trustee of Eritrea and entrusted the administration of it
 lekin jis ithiopia ko eritrea kii jimmedaari saunpi gai 10 saal ke bheetar laalach main aakar usne uske hisse ko jabaran apane desh main shaamil kar liya
 The freedom struggle of Eritrea started from here which ended in 1991
 1993 main refrendom ke jariye inhen aazaadee naseeb hui

 saavant ke vakil shishir tandon ne daleel di ki nichali adaalat ne mukademe kii sunwaayee shuru kar di he or ‘maamle ke tathyon or ricard main darj samagriyon ke sambandh main bina soche-samajhe’ samman jari kar diya
 The court adjourned the hearing of the case
 adaalat ne kaha ki duusare paksh se jawaab milane ke baad maamle par vichaar kiye jane kii aavashyaktaa he
 Sawant's TV show has been mired in controversy many times
 sho main abhadra bhashaa kaa istemaal kiye jane ko lekar shikaayat ke baad soochna evam prasaaran mantralay ke disha-nirdesh ke maddenjar use prime time se hataakar der raat main dikhaaya jane laga tha
 The main accused in the Unnao case and burning the victim alive was granted conditional bail by the court last month
 adaalat ne apni shart main kaha tha ki aaropee gavaahon ko prabhavit karne kii koshish nahin karegaa
 But the 23-year-old victim was burnt by five people including the main accused of rape early Thursday
 kareeb 90 pratishat tak jhulas chuki yuvati ko air ambulance ke jariye dilli laayaa gaya tha or yahaan safadarajang aspataal main bhartee karaayaa gaya tha
 He succumbed late Friday night while undergoing treatment
 peedita ke saath pichley saal disambar main balaatkaar kiya gaya tha
 Shivam Trivedi, one of the two accused, was granted bail on November 25 by the Lucknow bench of the Allahabad High Court
 iske thik 10 din baad usne anya chaar logon ke saath milakar peedita ke upar kerosine chhidak kar aag laga di thi
 Earlier, while granting bail, the court said, "the applicant will not try to influence the witnesses or tamper with the evidence of the case
" iske saath hi vah anyathaa jamaanat kii swatantraaa kaa durupyog karne kii bhi koshish nahin karegaa
 However, the bail plea was opposed by the public prosecutor
 vakil ne court ko bataaya tha ki do varsh pehle peedita ke saath balaatkaar hua or aropiyon ke dabaav ke chalate hi abhi tak uski shikaayat bhi darj nahin hui thi
 On Saturday, after the post mortem, the victim's body has been sent to her home in Unnao
 postmortem main report main kaha gaya he ki uski maut gambhir rup se jalane ke kaaran hui he
 At the same time, the victim's family refused to perform the last rites until the Chief Minister met them and assured them that justice would be done to them within a week
 peedita ke pita ne telugana police dwaara chaar balaatkaar ke aropiyon kii hatya kaa zikr karte hue kaha ki unki beti ke aropiyon ko bhi 'goli maar di jaani chahie
 ' silsilaa badalte rishton kaa in dinon charchaa main he

 ab serial ishkbaaj main omkara kaa kirdaar nibhaane vaale kunal jaisingh ke silsilaa main lead role nibhaane kii khabaren hai
 The current season stars Shakti Arora, Aditi Sharma and Kinshuk Mahajan in the lead roles
 in dinon sho main kunal-mauli-ishan ke bich jabardast trek dekhne ko mil rahaa he

 unki life par focus rahegaa

 twitor par unhone isaki jaankaree di

 post likhte hue shakti ne kaha, ''alavida kahana hameshaa dukhad hota he, lekin mujhe khushi he ki main sho silsilaa
 
 
 Taking a lot of memories from ab nai shuruyaat ke liye bhi taiyaar hum
 Cheers to the entire team of # Silsila
 '' In his life of seventy-five years, Farooq Abdullah has ruled Jammu and Kashmir for 12 years in five terms
 unke 42 varshiya bete umr abdulla kaa bataur mukhyamantri yah teesraa saal he
 Farooq's father Sheikh Abdullah spent most of his life in jail, sometimes by Maharaja Hari Singh, sometimes by the Indian government
 iske baavjood ve teen kaarykaal main 12 saal tak rajya ke mukhyamantri rahe
 On a cold December morning, Farooq met us at his residence at 11, Teenmurti Lane, between peacocks and a blue-eyed hide and seeker
 umr abhi-abhi jammu se aae hai or turant skool se laute apane donon bhaanjon se mil rahe hai (bahan sara or unke pati sachin payalat ke bachche)
 Omar says that Farooq is far more sociable and frank and if you "lock him in a room with books and music" you will be able to see his true form
 ” umr, khud apane shabdon main, utane hi udaar hai, lekin ekant premi hai
 Omar is thankful to his father that in his own way, he is letting him run the rule of Jammu and Kashmir, not directing him, as can be seen in some cases
 faruk kaa maananaa he ki 2010 main 117 logon kii maut ne umr ko ek 'behatar insaan’ banaaya
 Omar says that he does not refrain from hard work and does not intend to go anywhere
 india today kii editorcaveri bamazaior senior editorpriya sahagalane jammu or kashmir ke sabase mushkil halaat kii gavaah rahi do peedhishon ke bich behtareen samvaad ko apni kalam se darj kiya he
 • You remained in power for 12 years and Omar is the Chief Minister for three years
 tab or ab ke kashmir ke bich kya fark he?faruk abdulla oh, vah kashmir main bade badlaavon kaa daur tha
 My people were killed, my workers were killed, my ministers were blown up with an IED (emotive Explosive Device)
 unhone mujhe maarane kii manshaa se assembly par bhi hamalaa kiya
 But the good thing is that the Government of India and the people here stood by me
 maine 1990 main istipha diya or sabase kharaab daur kii shuruyaat 1991 main hui
 Many felt that the situation would not improve and Kashmir would go out of our hands
 lekin 2002 main chijen badalani shuru huin
 • What kind of changes? Farooq We have confronted terrorism
 ham kamjor nahin pade, hamane kaha ki koi or tarika nahin he, hamen laduya hi hoga
 The army supported us
 phir maine ekikrut kaman kii shuruyaat kii
 Pakistan then realized that terrorism itself was going against him and was having a bad effect
 9 / 11 ke baad hi duniya ko mahasoos hua ki aatankwaad ab global khatra ban chukaa he
 • The way Omar has worked for the last three years, what do you think? Farooq Umar's worst phase was 2010
 jab 117 yuvaaon kii maut hui thi
 • He came to you for advice at that time? Farooq is not a question of advice
 jab yah hua, to ve tuutane kii kagaar par the
 Only friends with him and his courage
 khuda kaa shukr he vah samay biit gaya
 They took a lesson and they are what they are today
 umr mujhe nahin lagata ki desh main kahin bhi kisi rajya ke str par itani badi jimmedaari he
 There are many reasons for this
 kisi bhi rajya main aisi vividhta nahin jo jammu or kashmir main he
 The impact of foreign policy with India's neighbors and not on a state as much as in the case of Jammu and Kashmir
 kahin bhi itani satta virdohi takatein kaam nahin karti hai
 • How has Omar changed? How do you see them today? Farooq i think that the events of the summer of 2010 have greatly increased their understanding of politics, they have told how things should be
 ve ek behatar insaan bane hai
 better than ever
 usee daur se ubarkar ve netaa ban sake
 • Has there ever been a time when you have sat with them and talked to them without asking Omar? Farooq yes
 masalan, 2009 main sex sambandhi aaropon par jab umr ne assembly main istipha de diya tha (vipakshi pidipi ne 2009 main aarope lagaaya tha ki 2006 ke ek sex scandle main mukhyamantri shaamil the)
 i advised him, "how can you dare to do this?" You have become the Chief Minister with the support of the alliance and if you have to do anything like this, then you should talk to the coalition partner first
 ” main ukhd gaya tha
 Then he said to me, "but Dad, how will i face my children?" How do i tell them that i am not what they said? How do i get in front of my friends and wife? " i said, "I can understand, but if you have done it now, you will have to face it again
" thik he, governor ko jaanch karne do
 Till then don't take any big step
 ” ve kaaphi bhaavnaatmak hai
 • How was your relationship with Walid? Farooq was mostly brought up by his mother
 pita to aksar jail main rahete the
 But he kept strict discipline
 mujhe unka ek baar kaa thappad yaad he
 • And your relationship with Omar? Farooq i have been quite soft
 meri bivi ne inhen bada kiya
 Punctuality and discipline of money is found from there
 sanavar ke laurence skool ne inhen pairon par khadaa hona sikhaaya
 • When he expressed his desire to enter politics, were you shocked? Farooq She (wife Molly) has been a witness to my life
 kehane ke liye jindagi hoti he bas—aap savere nikal jate hai or raat main lautate hai
 Where to eat, where not to eat to jab umr ne raajnneeti karne kii ichha jataai, maine unhen phone karke bataaya, ''mal, ab kya karen?” unhone kaha, ''ve chaahate hai to unhen kismat aajamaane dijie
 i said, 'goodluck'
 2002 main jab ye haare the, inhone badi himmat se uskaa saamana kiya tha
 Omar i do not think my father would have been surprised
 jab chijen inke hisaab se nahin chalati hai, to maa se bachane kaa yah inkaa tarika hota he
 • What was the effect of the defeat on you in the 2002 election? Omar, i think it is not right to sit in a chair in 2002
 mujhe iske kaaran rajya ke bare main or zyada jaanane-samajhane kaa mauka mila
 In the case of personal growth, it is not that you learn them only by losing elections, you can also learn by winning
 lekin isane mujhe vinamrata kii sikh di
 i was too hasty in public announcements, having a chance to fix it while in opposition
 or mujhe lagata he ki sabase bada sabak yah mila ki vipaksh main rahete hue janata se aapkaa sampark sidhaa or jamini rahata he kyonki aapke paas sarkari helicopter kii suvidha nahin hoti
 There is no better way to know the geography of your state than that you reached here by driving here and there, this is what i did
 isse mujhe jamini sabak seekhney ko mili, log kaise sochate hai
 • Would have been happier in hotel business? Omar i doubt how boring that would have been! • Understood Kashmiri mentality? Can Umar make such a claim? i share that mindset myself and see complexities within me as well
 jo log 2010 kii garmiyon main baghawat kar rahe the unhone baad main vot die
 • What about the Kashmiri people who talk about lack of trust? Omar can you blame them? Look at what they have gone through in the last 20-22 years
 har santhaan jis par unhone bharosa kiya, naakaam rahaa he, chaahe adaalatein hon, police ho, sarkaar, civil sosayadi yaa phir siyaasi netritv
 • Do you see your sons as future leaders? Umar honestly, no
 mujhe ummid he ki neshnal conference kaa netritv karne vaala main aakhri abdulla hum
 The party does not stop with anyone coming and going
 vah aage badhkar apana netaa chun hi leti he
 Even if my children enter politics, i would hope that by then i have left politics and they can make their own way
 srilanka ke khilaaf test siries jeetne ke baad ab pakistan team kii nazar vanade series par he
 The first ODI of the 5 ODI series between the two countries will be played on 11 July i
e
 tomorrow in Dambulla
 agar pakistani team series jitati he to wo champions trophy main qualifaai kar jaaegi
 Led by misbah-ul-haq, the team won the Test series 2–1 and won the Test series in Sri Lanka 9 years later
 aakiri test main younus khan or shaan masood ne shandaar shatak banaaya jisaki vajah se pakistan ne 377 ran kaa lakshya aasaani se hasil kiya
 Azhar Ali is the captain in place of Misbah in odis, while Younis and Masood have not been selected in the ODI team
 azar ali ke kandhon par ahm zimmedaari he kyonki isisi ranking main 9wein sthaan par maujuud pakistan ke saamne england main hone vaale aath deshon kii champions trophy main qualifaai karne kii chunauti he
 The ODI captain of the team said, "one day series with Sri Lanka is very important for our team and we will try to win by doing well here
" ham muqaabale ke liye puri tarah se taiyaar hai''
 The captain may be talking about getting ready for the series, but the team's performance in odis has not been good for the last few months
 march main world cap main team quarter-final main australia se harkar toornament se baahar hui thi
 Bangladesh then whitewashed Pakistan 3–0 at their home
 azhar ali kii team ko kuch raahat apane gharelu series main zimbabwe ko haraakar kuch raahat zarur mili
 Talking about the fitness of the players, Wahab Riaz is still not fit
 wahaab ko test series ke dauraan haath main chot lagi thi

 team main tej gendbaaz mohammad irafaan kii chot se vaapasi zarur hui he, jo world cap ke dauraan qamar main chot kii vajah se baahar hue the
 The ODI series will feature two new batsmen
 22 saal ke mukhtaar ahamed or 29 saal ke bilal asif
 The comments duusari taraf srilankai team mahela jayavardhane or kumaar sangakara ke vanade se sanyas lene ke baad pehla vanade series khelegi
 Both the players retired from odis after the World Cup in australia-new Zealand
 srilankai team kii captaini anjalo maitheus ke haathon main he or isamen 6 khilaadi test team se hai
 The series between Sri Lanka and Pakistan will be played according to the new ODI rules of the ICC
 series kaa doosraa vanade 15 july, teesraa vanade 19 july, chauthaa vanade 22 july or aakiri vanade 26 july ko khelaa jayega
 It will be the first ODI match of the series while the remaining four odis will be day-night matches
 misbah-ul-haq kii aguwai main team ne test series main 2-1 se jeet hasil kiya or 9 saal baad srilanka main test series apane naam kiya
 In the last Test, Younis Khan and Shaan Masood scored a brilliant century, due to which Pakistan easily achieved the target of 377 runs
 vanade main misbah kii jagah azhar ali captain hai, to younus or masood ko vanade team main nahin chunaa gaya he
 Azar Ali has an important responsibility on his shoulders as Pakistan, ranked 9th in the ICC rankings, has the challenge of qualifying for the eight-nation Champions Trophy to be held in England
 team ke vanade captain ne kaha,''srilanka ke saath vanade series hamaari team ke liye kaafii mahatvapurn he or ham yahaan acha pradarshan kar jeetne kii koshish karenge
 We are all set for the fight ''
 captain bhale hi series ke liye taiyaar hone kii baat kar rahe ho, lekin pichley kuch maheenon se vanade main team kaa pradarshan acha nahin rahaa he
